            More from our Chairman and Group CEO
        </span><span class="accordion__arrowIcon"></span></button><div class="accordion__contentWrapper container container--stackedContent container--stackedContent-large verticalshrink__base verticalshrink__base--collapsed verticalshrink__base--transition" aria-hidden="true" aria-labelledby="1533840274" id="c1533840274" role="region"><div class="accordion__content
                    container__content"><div data-nc="GridContext" class="basecomponent basecomponent__base textimage textimage__base textimagegridcontext__context--extra-narrow textimage__context textimage__context--generous" data-gridcontext-name="textimagegridcontext" data-gridcontext-context="generous"><div class="highlighting__base highlighting__base--default " id="textimage-2142986259" style="--imagecomponent-width: 100%"><div class="textimage__richtext richtext__base  "><p>The year 2024 marked another 12 months of change for UBS and the world we live in. In the first full year since our acquisition of Credit Suisse, we transitioned from stabilizing a precarious situation to making significant strides toward integration. We achieved all our key acquisition-related milestones on or ahead of schedule and accelerated the transition to growth. UBS is now stronger, more diversified and better positioned strategically to benefit both our clients and our shareholders in a rapidly changing world.</p><p>We support most of the recommendations made by the Swiss Federal Council to strengthen the resilience of the financial center, including the introduction of a Senior Manager Regime and a Public Liquidity Backstop. We share the Federal Councils strong commitment to a global Swiss financial center.</p><p>As Switzerlands leading financial institution, the continued success of UBS and Switzerlands position as a global financial center are inextricably linked for mutual prosperity.<br><strong>Colm Kelleher, Chairman</strong></p><p>Through the integration of Credit Suisse, we have strengthened our position as the largest truly global wealth manager and the leading bank in Switzerland. We have broadened our geographical footprint and enhanced our range of products and services including in our Asset Management and Investment Bank divisions. This diversification has made us even stronger than before the acquisition. Our strength and stability set us apart in times of uncertainty around global trade, geopolitics, inflation and central bank policies.</p><p>Even as our global reach expands, we remain steadfast in our commitment to act as an engine of growth and prosperity in Switzerland, our home market. As a leading provider of credit to Swiss households and corporate clients, we granted or renewed over CHF 70 billion of loans in Switzerland last year out of a total book of around CHF 350 billion, helping our communities to prosper in ways that benefit both households and businesses and our shareholders.</p><p>We are confident about the future and the value we deliver. With our clear strategy and progress on our integration, we are well positioned to offer outstanding client experiences and grow sustainably, enabling us to generate higher returns on capital and provide you, our valued shareholders, with attractive returns.<br><strong>Sergio Ermotti, Group CEO</strong></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="basecomponent As a result, UBS realizes a net gain of USD 0.3 billion in Q1 2024, while Credit Suisse AG expects a net loss of USD 0.9 billion due to different accounting adjustments and provisions.</p></div><div class="basecomponent basecomponent__base linklistnewlook linklistnewlook__base"><div class="linklistnewlook__context linklistnewlook__context--narrow" data-nc="GridContext" data-gridcontext-name="linklistnewlookgridcontext" data-gridcontext-context="narrow"><div class="linklistnewlook__wrapper linklistnewlook__wrapper--standard"><div class="linklistnewlook__listItem link"><a href="https://www.ubs.com/global/en/media/display-page-ndp/en-20240327-apollo.html" rel="noopener" class="externalLink  listitem__link listitem__link--linklist svgicon--hoverTrigger listitem__link--internal link__base" target="_blank"><span class="listitem__text">

This donation provides USD 10 million for direct funding and USD 15 million to match clients and employees contributions. The funds support initiatives in health, education and climate. /* Keep/Remove URL Query Parameters (UBSANASUP-1003) */
window.keepParams = function(key, sourceURL, options) {
  if(typeof key == "undefined"){
    key = ["campID", "intCampID", "gclid", "msclkid", "s_kwcid", "at_preview", "sprinklrpostid", "codes", "adformclickid"];
  }
  if(typeof sourceURL != "string"){
    return ""; 
  }
  try{
    var returnURL    = sourceURL.split("?")[0],
        queryString  = (sourceURL.indexOf("?") !== -1) ? sourceURL.split("?")[1] : "",
        params_arr   = [],
        new_params   = [],
        paramsToKeep = key,
        paramValue   = "",
        paramKey,
        emailPattern = /(^(.+)@(.+)\.(.+).*$)/;
    if(queryString !== "") {
      params_arr = queryString.split("&");
      params_arr.forEach(function(element){
        var keyValue = element.split("=");
        paramKey     = keyValue[0].toLowerCase();
        for(i=1; i<keyValue.length; i++){
          if (emailPattern.test(keyValue[i])){
            keyValue.splice(i,1,"input_hidden");
            element = keyValue.join("=");
          }
        }
        paramsToKeep.forEach(function(e){
          elm = e.toLowerCase();
          switch(options){
            case "startswith":
              if (paramKey.indexOf(elm) == 0) {
                new_params.push(element);
              }
              break;
            case "contains":
              if (paramKey.indexOf(elm) > -1) {
                new_params.push(element);
              }
              break;
            case "equals":
              if (paramKey === elm) {
                new_params.push(element);
              }
              break;
            default:
              if (paramKey === elm) {
                new_params.push(element);
              }
          }
        })
      })
      if (new_params.length) {
        returnURL = returnURL + "?" + new_params.join("&");
      }
    }
    return returnURL;
  }catch(e){
    console.error(e.message);
    return returnURL + "?errMsg=" +e.message;
  }
}
/* END: Keep/Remove URL Query Parameters (UBSANASUP-1003) */

/* Keep/Remove validate if the string contains Email ID OR Phone number (UBSANASUP-1003) */
window.vaildateEmailPhoneNumber = function(value) {
  try {
    var emailPattern = /(^(.+)@(.+)\.(.+).*$)|(^\d{9,}$)|(^(\+).*(\s)*(\d{6,})$)/;
    var phonePattern = /\d{6}/
    if (emailPattern.test(value) || phonePattern.test(value)) {
        value = "input_hidden";
    }
    return value;
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e.message);
    return e.message;
  }
}
/* END: validate if the string contains Email ID OR Phone number (UBSANASUP-1003) */

/* Clean XDM and Data Attributes if their values are empty */
window.cleanObject = function(uncleanObject) {
  //  function cleanObject(uncleanObject) {
  for (let key in uncleanObject) {
    if (uncleanObject.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
      const value = uncleanObject[key];
      if (value === undefined || value === null || value === "") {
        delete uncleanObject[key];
      } else if (typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
        cleanObject(value);
        if (Object.keys(value).length === 0) {
          delete uncleanObject[key];
        }
      } else if (Array.isArray(value)) {
        uncleanObject[key] = value.filter(item => item !== undefined && item !== null && item !== "");
        if (uncleanObject[key].length === 0) {
          delete uncleanObject[key];
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return uncleanObject;
}
/* END: Clean XDM and Data Attributes if their values are empty */

/* Find the closest element of a clicked link */
/* Used in file download and exit link tracking to populate activitymap regions */
window.findClosestAttribute = function(element) {
  const selectors = ["id", "header", "main", "footer", "nav"];
  let currentElement = element.closest("[id], header, main, footer, nav, [role='region'][aria-label]");
  if (currentElement) {
    // Check if it's an element with one of the attributes
    for (const attr of selectors) {
      if (currentElement.hasAttribute(attr)) {
        return currentElement.getAttribute(attr);
      }
    }
    // Check for the aria-label attribute when role="region"
    if (currentElement.getAttribute("role") === "region" && currentElement.hasAttribute("aria-label")) {
      return currentElement.getAttribute("aria-label");
    }
  }
  return null; // No matching attribute found
}
/* END: Find the closest element of a clicked link */

window.adobeDataLayer = window.adobeDataLayer || [];
window.trackingQueue  = window.trackingQueue  || [];
var trackedStatus  = window.trackingType   || "";

/* Set Adobe consent based on user's cookie consent */
if(_satellite.getVar("CC:isThirdPartyTracking") === "true"){
  if(trackedStatus === "thirdParty"){
    _satellite.track("updateConsent");
    _satellite.logger.log("##### All tags are already fired!")
  }else if(trackedStatus === "firstParty"){
    window.trackingType = "thirdParty";
    _satellite.track("updateConsent");
    _satellite.track("marketingTags");
    _satellite.logger.log("##### Only first party tags already fired, thirdPartyTracking now allowed, marketingTags fired...")
  } else{
    window.trackingType = "thirdParty";
    _satellite.track("updateConsent");
    _satellite.track("analyticsPageLoad");
    _satellite.track("marketingTags");
    _satellite.logger.log("##### thirdPartyTracking allowed, analyticsPageLoad & marketingTags are fired...")
  }
} else if(_satellite.getVar("CC:isFirstPartyTracking") === "true"){
  if(trackedStatus === "firstParty" || trackedStatus === "thirdParty"){
    _satellite.track("updateConsent");
    _satellite.logger.log("##### First party tags already fired, rule condition failed!")
  } else{
    window.trackingType = "firstParty";
    _satellite.track("updateConsent");
    _satellite.track("analyticsPageLoad");
    _satellite.logger.log("##### firstPartyTracking allowed, analyticsPageLoad fired...")
  }
} else{
  _satellite.track("updateConsent");
  _satellite.logger.log("##### No tracking is allowed, no events fired!");
}
/* END: Set Adobe consent based on user's cookie consent */
